	// This event handler on the window is invoked whenever a browser window is brought
	// into focus, either by switching tabs or windows. This would also be called when
	// the application is first called.

	YAHOO.util.Event.on(window, "focus", logOffStaleUser);

	// This function checks if the user as shown by the page header is the same as the logged in user in the session
	// If not, it invokes the log out url. The user at the time of page load is available in the span element with ID
	// pageuser and last logged in user is available in the cookie "lastUser"

	function logOffStaleUser () {

		var pageUser = "";
		var spanEl = document.getElementById("pageuser");
		if (null != spanEl && null != spanEl.firstChild) {
			pageUser = spanEl.firstChild.nodeValue;
		}

		var loggedInUser = readCookie("lastUser");

		// function window.atob used to decode the string.
		// escape the whole string and then encode it.

		}

	function changeRole(selEl) {
		var form = document.createElement('form');

		form.setAttribute('action', 'ImpersonationAction.do');
		form.setAttribute('method', 'GET');
		form.setAttribute('name', 'roleform');

		var roleName = selEl.options[selEl.selectedIndex].text;

		var method = makeHidden('method', 'method', 'changeRole') ;
		var roleIdEl = makeHidden('userRoleId', 'userRoleId', selEl.value) ;
		var roleNameEl = makeHidden('roleName', 'roleName', roleName);

		form.appendChild(method);
		form.appendChild(roleIdEl);
		form.appendChild(roleNameEl);
		document.body.appendChild(form);
		document.roleform.submit();
		return true;
	}

	function changeCenter(selEl) {
		var form = document.createElement('form');

		form.setAttribute('action', 'ImpersonationAction.do');
		form.setAttribute('method', 'GET');
		form.setAttribute('name', 'centerform');

		var centerName = selEl.options[selEl.selectedIndex].text;

		var method = makeHidden('method', 'method', 'changeCenter') ;
		var centerIdEl = makeHidden('modifiedCenterId', 'modifiedCenterId', selEl.value) ;
		var centerNameEl = makeHidden('modifiedCenterName', 'modifieldCenterName', centerName);

		form.appendChild(method);
		form.appendChild(centerIdEl);
		form.appendChild(centerNameEl);
		document.body.appendChild(form);
		document.centerform.submit();
		return true;

	}
</script>

<script>
	if (true) {
		YAHOO.util.Event.addListener(document.forms.BillSearchForm, "submit", validateSearchTagForm);
	}
	function validateSearchTagForm(event) {
		if (!doSearch()) {
			YAHOO.util.Event.stopEvent(event);
			return false;
		}
		// 1) onchange of saved favourite search it submits the page with setting the method to getMySearch and action
		// 		as SearchAction.do. it will returns result list with the selected favourite search criteria.
		// 2) now clinck on the browser back button it will loads the previous page. with setting the methos as
		// 		as getMySearch only. now if user clicks on search button it will give error because getMySearch method
		//		will not be there in the corresponging action.
		// since _method and _searchMethod contains the same values. set the _searchMethod value to the _method parameter
		// so that it will forward to the correct method. refer BUG : 23040
		var searchForm = document.forms.BillSearchForm;
		searchForm._method.value = searchForm._searchMethod.value;

		return true;
	}
</script>
